{"nick":"GreenJello","message":"express for everything","date":"2015-09-24T00:30:27.386Z","type":"message"}
{"nick":"joepie91","message":"ones, where possible - using 20 modules of 5 lines each is perfectly okay. use require() in your code to load a module - if just a name, it looks in your npm-installed modules for that project. if a path (relative or absolute), it loads the specified path. to create a require()able .js file, simply make the file assign something to module.exports - whatever is assigned to module.exports is what will come out of require()ing it (as a return value)","date":"2015-09-24T00:30:28.397Z","type":"message"}
